***демобилизовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:демобилизовать.html>демобилизова́ть</a> (17857)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">démobiliser</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демобилизовать.html>демобилизова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">demobilizovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">демобилизо́вывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to demobilize <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. troops</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to discharge</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***демократичный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:демократичный.html>демократи́чный</a> (20705)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">démocrat(ique)</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́чный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демократичный.html>демократи́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">demokratíčnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>simple, unpretentious, humble; like or in the manner of the common man
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2002</b>,  Ольга Кабанова,  “Легко <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>века</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:юбилей.html>Юбиле́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:театральный.html>театра́льного</a> дома”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Izvestia" class="extiw" title="w:Izvestia">Izvestia</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оно.html>оно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вызывающий.html>вызыва́юще</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:демократичный.html>демократи́чно</a></b> — <a href = vnd.unilang:никакой.html>никако́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:привычный.html>привы́чной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:роскошь.html>ро́скоши</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:красный.html>кра́сного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бархат.html>ба́рхата</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ложе.html>лож</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">onó býlo vyzyvájušče <b>demokratíčno</b> — nikakój privýčnoj róskoši, krásnovo bárxata, lož</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">it was provocatively <b>simple</b>—none of the usual luxury, red velvet, or boxes</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>affordable or accessible for the ordinary person</li>
<li>egalitarian</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:демон.html>де́мон</a> (6514)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демон.html>де́мон</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">démon</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демон.html>де́мона</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демон.html>де́моны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демон.html>де́монов</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:демонстрационный.html>демонстрацио́нный</a> (25563)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демонстрация.html>демонстра́ция</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">demonstrácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́нный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демонстрационный.html>демонстрацио́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">demonstraciónnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)демонстрацио́ннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)демонстрацио́нней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> demonstration <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">public display, political protest, or show of military force</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:демонстрационный.html>демонстрацио́нный</a></b> полёт</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>demonstraciónnyj</b> poljót</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>demonstration</b> flight</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>demonstrative</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> diversionary action</li></ol>

<ol><li>частичн.: <a href = vnd.unilang:показательный.html>показа́тельный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:представительский.html>представи́тельский</a></li>

***демонстрация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:демонстрация.html>демонстра́ция</a> (5544)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">демонстр(и́ровать)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">demonstr(írovatʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ция</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демонстрация.html>демонстра́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">demonstrácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демонстрация.html>демонстра́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демонстрация.html>демонстра́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демонстрация.html>демонстра́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>demonstration <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">show, display</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>demonstration <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">march, protest</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устраивать.html>устра́ивать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:демонстрация.html>демонстра́ции</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ustráivatʹ <b>demonstrácii</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to organize <b>demonstrations</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>demonstration <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">show of military force</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mass procession</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> diversionary action</li></ol>

***демонстрировавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:демонстрировать.html>демонстри́ровавший</a> (4750)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***демонтировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:демонтировать.html>демонти́ровать</a> (24673)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">démonter</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:демонтировать.html>демонти́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">demontírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to dismantle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to disband, to abolish</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">denʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ёк</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:денек.html>денёк</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">denjók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:денек.html>денька́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:денек.html>деньки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:денек.html>денько́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">denʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: day
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1885</b>,  Антон Павлович <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Pavlovich Chekhov</a>),  “<a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%94%D0%B0%D1%87%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%BA%D0%B8_(%D0%A7%D0%B5%D1%85%D0%BE%D0%B2)" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Дачники (Чехов)"><a href = vnd.unilang:дачник.html>Да́чники</a></a>  | A Country Cottage | ”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:осколок.html>Оско́лки</a></cite>  | <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fragments_(magazine)" class="extiw" title="w:Fragments (magazine)">Fragments</a></cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колоть.html>ко́ля</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:костя.html>ко́стя</a>, ни́на, <a href = vnd.unilang:фифа.html>фи́фа</a> ... <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>де́ти</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:целовать.html>целу́йте</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кузен.html>кузе́на</a> са́шу! <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выводок.html>вы́водком</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:денек.html>денька́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:надеяться.html>наде́юсь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> стесни́м? <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>Ты</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:пожалуйста.html>пожа́луйста</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:церемония.html>церемо́нии</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kólja, Kóstja, Nína, Fífa ... déti! Celújte kuzɛ́na Sášu! Vse k tebé, vsem vývodkom, i <b>denʹká</b> na tri, na četýre. Nadéjusʹ, ne stesním? Ty, požálujsta, bez ceremónii.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Kolya, Kostya, Nina, Fifa ... children! Kiss your cousin Sasha! Here we all are, with our whole brood, for three or four <b>short days</b>. I hope we won't be crowding you? Please don't go to any trouble.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1968</b>,  Александр Исаевич Солженицын (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aleksandr_Solzhenitsyn" class="extiw" title="w:Aleksandr Solzhenitsyn">Aleksandr Isayevich Solzhenitsyn</a>),  chapter 8, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> кругле <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвом</a></cite>  | <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/In_the_First_Circle" class="extiw" title="w:In the First Circle">In the First Circle</a></cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>Но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>тако́го</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:денек.html>денька́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> «ю́нкерсы» пики́рующие <a href = vnd.unilang:чуть.html>чуть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>ча́сти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рва́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> орло́м — <a href = vnd.unilang:никак.html>ника́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>могу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:воссоздать.html>воссозда́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удовольствие.html>удово́льствия</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">No ot takóvo <b>denʹká</b>, kogdá “Júnkersy” pikírujuščije čutʹ ne na části menjá rváli pod Orlóm — nikák ja ne mogú vossozdátʹ v sebé udovólʹstvija.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">But from that <b>godawful day</b>, when divebombing Junkers nearly tore me to pieces near Orel, I can't recall any sort of pleasure.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***день.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> (80)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дьнь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dĭnĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dьnь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">day</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">denʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дня</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>day, daytime
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>де́нь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>dénʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">per day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>ве́сь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>де́нь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vésʹ <b>dénʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">all day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>де́нь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>днём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dénʹ</b> za dnjóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">day after day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>де́нь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ото.html>ото</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дня́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dénʹ</b> oto <b>dnjá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from day to day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>де́нь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рождение.html>рожде́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dénʹ roždénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">birthday</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>днём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dnjom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">by day, during the day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изо.html>и́зо</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дня́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>де́нь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ízo <b>dnjá</b> v <b>dénʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">day by day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дня́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>dnjáx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the other day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тих</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дня́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na étix <b>dnjáx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">one of these days</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рабочий.html>рабо́чий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>де́нь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rabóčij <b>dénʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">work day</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>afternoon, early evening
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> 3 <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часа́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дня́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v 3 časá <b>dnjá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">at 3 o’clock in the afternoon</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> 7 <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дня́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v 7 časóv <b>dnjá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">at 7 o’clock in the evening</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">днёвка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dnjóvka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***деньга.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>деньга</a> (22848)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>де́ньга</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dénʹga</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деньга.html>деньг</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">numismatics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> denga <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an old Russian coin</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This word, with the stress on the first syllable, is the origin of the modern word <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dénʹgi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">money</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which is now only used in plural. <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>деньга́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">denʹgá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with the stress on the 2nd syllable is used colloquially in modern Russian and often considered slang or non-standard.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>деньга́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">denʹgá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>деньги́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>деньги́</a></i>, <i>genitive plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деньга.html>деньг</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> money, dough</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> coin, note</li></ol>

***деньги.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>деньги</a> (193)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> source, cf. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kazakh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kazakh language">Kazakh</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="kk">теңге</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="kk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">teñge</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bashkir_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bashkir language">Bashkir</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ba">тәңкә</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ba-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">täñkä</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First used in the singular form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>де́ньга</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>деньга́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dénʹga, denʹgá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ancient coin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, preserved in modern Russian as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>деньга́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">denʹgá</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">money, dough <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dénʹgi</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́нег</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>money
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>сто́ит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>больши́х</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́нег</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto stóit bolʹšíx <b>déneg</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It costs a lot of <b>money</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
